    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }

  <span id="freeText8613809639480961511" style="display:none">Life outside of her house was a new experience for Della Sloane. The dark secrets of her past weren’t something she ever intended to share with anyone. They would never understand. No one would ever get close enough to find out. There was always a chance she’d go crazy sooner than they expected…<br /><br />Woods Kerrington had never been one to be attracted to fragile females. They seemed like too much work. He wasn’t in it for the work just the pleasure. A night full of naughty fun had been exactly what was on his mind when he’d laid eyes on the hot little number that didn’t know how to pump gas and needed some help.<br /><br />What he didn’t know was she was as fragile as they came.<br />The carefree girl who spoke her mind and didn’t care what the world thought of her was more breakable than he could ever imagine…</span>

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5604583-aestas-book-blog?shelf=book-1-of-my-fav-series">book-1-of-my-fav-series</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536749980" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8798213217463798844"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688374._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b> <i> <blockquote> “I’ll be whatever she needs me to be. I can’t walk away from her, I tried. I’m hooked.” </blockquote> </i> </b><br/><b> Each book from Abbi Glines is more addictive than the last! </b><br/><br/>I read Twisted Perfection in one sitting and was glued to the page, unable to put it down. It was hot, steamy and sometimes a little dirty *winks*, with a fast-paced plot and lovable characters. It’s a little darker than the Too Far books, but I’d still actually consider it a relatively light read.<br/><br/>Having lived her whole life with a mentally ill</span>
  <span id="freeText8798213217463798844" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688374._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> <i> <blockquote> “I’ll be whatever she needs me to be. I can’t walk away from her, I tried. I’m hooked.” </blockquote> </i> </b><br><b> Each book from Abbi Glines is more addictive than the last! </b><br><br>I read Twisted Perfection in one sitting and was glued to the page, unable to put it down. It was hot, steamy and sometimes a little dirty *winks*, with a fast-paced plot and lovable characters. It’s a little darker than the Too Far books, but I’d still actually consider it a relatively light read.<br><br>Having lived her whole life with a mentally ill mother who, out of her personal fears, kept her inside all the time, Della finds her life unexpectedly changed when her mother dies. Three years later, she is still struggling to find herself and decides a road trip is the best answer. So she throws all caution and inhibitions to the wind and heads out. At her first rest stop, she meets Woods.. And ohhhh my do they have chemistry. She isn’t looking to stick around, but she can’t help but take up his offer of dinner… and more.<br><br>Woods has enough going on in his life. Too much. He’s being pressured from his family to marry a woman he dislikes for the ‘good of the family business’. It’s either that, or he loses his part of the business and everything he’s worked towards his whole life. The thought makes him miserable but, he wants the job desperately and so is just trying to delay the inevitable marriage.<br><br>So when he sees Della at the gas station, he sees perfection. She is exactly what he needs right now. A fun time that would drive away afterwards – no strings.<br><br>What neither of them counted on was their hearts getting attached and despite the fact that they both drive off after their night together, fate soon crosses their paths again and this time, they’re not leaving each other.<br><br><b> <i> <blockquote> “My future was about to be thrown off track because Della Sloane was under my skin and I had to have her.” </blockquote> </i> </b><br><br>Woods. Was. Delicious. Purely delicious!! And yummy. Very yummy. Ohhh and a bit of a dirty talker but he still called her sweetheart right from the start which was super sweet. He was protective and I loved that being around Della brought out his hothead caveman side. It was seriously swoony!<br><br>I really liked Della. She was broken in many ways but at the same time was really quite free. She may not have been experienced at relationships but she certainly wasn’t shy at going after what she wanted with Woods and I have to say it was refreshing to read her kind of character who on the one hand was like that while at the same time, really messed up inside. It was a cool mix. She had issues, but they didn’t take over every part of her life.<br><br>I don’t know a better way to describe Abbi’s books than by saying that reading them feels like watching a very well-written, addictive TV show. The scenes, they way their cut together, everything about them just makes me feel like I’m watching it happen right in front of me.<br><br>This book certainly brings on the angst in certain scenes!! Serious, serious angst. BUT! And here’s what I loved about it: the main angst (at least to me) is resolved in the first half of the book, leaving the second half to be focused quite a bit on Woods and Della sorting their relationship out, which I really enjoyed. That isn’t to say there isn’t angst in the second half, ‘cuz there is, but it’s a different kind (less nerve wracking, more focused on sorting issues out) and I appreciated the switch up.<br><br><b> <i> <blockquote> “You are mine. Do you hear me? You are mine, Della Sloane. I will take care of you. Nothing is taking you away from me. Nothing.” </blockquote> </i> </b><br><br>There is a bit of a love “square” going on for part of the book, but it was clear that Woods was never in love with the girl he was supposed to marry, it was more a question of him falling in love for the first time in his life and being put in position of having to choose “head or heart”? And while Della also connected with another guy she met on her road trip, her heart really always belonged to Woods.<br><br>That being said, their road to getting together was a fair bit bumpy, but, honestly, it wouldn’t have been nearly as much fun if the ride had been smooth, lol.<br><br>Della goes through some pretty hard issues in the book and I loved how supportive Woods was of everything. They were just a wonderful couple together.<br><br>And speaking them as a couple, this book was full of panty-ripping hotness. For real. As I mentioned, Woods has a bit of a dirty mouth and Della just loses it around so they’re a pretty explosive together. Hot, hot, HOT! Lol, sometimes, I’ll admit, it was borderline awkward in places to me, but most just plain freaking hot!<br><br>And I really have to give a bit of a shout-out to some of the awesome supporting men in this book. First to Tripp, who had better be getting his own damn book cuz that man has SWOON. I want more of him! And then also to Kent, who made my heart melt even though he was only in like two small scenes. Holy heart warming protectiveness!<br><br>For those of you wondering about cameos, Blaire does have a brief cameo but neither she nor Rush play a central part in the book. As much as I love their characters though, I didn’t miss them here. I was happy to see the book focused on Woods and Della.<br><br>The ending had me flipping pages like crazy. I knew it would all work out but that didn’t stop me from being worried, lol. You know how it is <br><br>To soothe your hearts, you should know that there is no relationship cliffhanger! The book ends in a good place relationship-wise. However, this is NOT a stand alone and there will be a sequel out in the fall, so there is a bit of a plot-related cliffy in that something happened at the end to make me want more of the story, but at the same time, it left them in a place where my heart could be happy to wait till the fall. At the end of the book, they are very much together as a couple. So, you will not want to throw your kindle at the wall. It’s all safe!! ♥<br><br>See?<br><br><b> <i> <blockquote> “Is she forever for you then? She’s worth throwing it all away?”…<br><br>“She’s it. No one else. She’s all I’m ever gonna want.” </blockquote> </i> </b><br><br>I loved the book and totally enjoyed spending my evening wrapped up in this world.<br><br><b> Definitely recommended if you are looking for something quick, hot, swoony, slightly angsty, fast-paced and addictive :) </b><br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><br>*******************<br><br><u> <b> TOO FAR &amp; PERFECTION SERIES READING ORDER!!! </b></u> <br><br>I know there's been a bit of confusion over these series' reading orders so hopefully this'll answer your questions:<br><br>Ok, so originally, Twisted Perfection was supposed to be the 3rd book in the TOO FAR series. The first two books were Fallen Too Far and Never Too Far. Those two books followed Rush and Blaire's story and then the original third book (Twisted Perfection) was supposed to be Woods', followed next by Grant's. <br><br>This all changed when, by popular demand, a third book "Forever Too Far" about Rush and Blaire was added to the TOO FAR series. After this change, Abbi Glines then separated the two series. <br><br>Now, the original series is the TOO FAR series, which now has a spin-off series that Twisted Perfection starts called the PERFECTION series. There will be a sequel to Twisted Perfection coming out this fall called Simple Perfection.<br><br>I'll list them all here in order so you can see:<br><br>TOO FAR SERIES - about Rush and Blaire<br><br>♥ #1 Fallen Too Far - out now<br>♥ #2 Never Too Far - out now<br>♥ #3 Forever Too Far - to be released late Summer 2013<br><br>PERFECTION SERIES (spin-off of TOO FAR) - about Woods and Della<br><br>♥ #1 Twisted Perfection --&gt; to be released today<br>♥ #2 Simple Perfection --&gt; to be released Fall 2013<br><br>You do not *have* to read the TOO FAR series to understand Twisted Perfection, but the whole world is the same so I'd recommend it if you can. I loved both Fallen Too Far and Never Too Far, so I'd say it would be good to read them, but not necessary.<br><br>Okay, hopefully that helps clear everything up :)<br><br><br>***************************<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688375._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>BLURB --&gt; <i> Life outside of her house was a new experience for Della Sloane. The dark secrets of her past weren’t something she ever intended to share with anyone. They would never understand. No one would ever get close enough to find out. Besides there was always a chance she’d go crazy sooner than they expected…<br><br>Woods Kerrington had never been one to be attracted to fragile females. They seemed like too much work. He wasn’t in it for the work just the pleasure. A night full of naughty fun had been exactly what was on his mind when he’d laid eyes on the hot little number that didn’t know how to pump gas and needed some help.<br><br>What he didn’t know was she was as fragile as they came.<br><br>The carefree girl who spoke her mind and didn’t care what the world thought of her was more breakable than he could ever imagine…<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></b></i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer544504469" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11241071680550822250"><br/><i>

</i> ~ Woods<br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688376._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Twisted Perfection</b> was again, an Abbi Glines story that I was unable to put down. It was a fun, sexy and light story that I VERY much enjoyed reading. I'd even go so far as to say that I loved it more than Rush and Blaire's story; mainly because I loved the main characters much, much more...<br/><br/><br/><b>Woods --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688377.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Della --</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688378.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Della Sloane</b> hasn't always had an easy life. Growing up with a mother who barely led her leav</span>
  <span id="freeText11241071680550822250" style="display:none"><br><i>
  <b>"I'll be whatever she needs me to be. I can't walk away from her; I tried. I'm hooked."</b>
</i> ~ Woods<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688376._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Twisted Perfection</b> was again, an Abbi Glines story that I was unable to put down. It was a fun, sexy and light story that I VERY much enjoyed reading. I'd even go so far as to say that I loved it more than Rush and Blaire's story; mainly because I loved the main characters much, much more...<br><br><br><b>Woods --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688377.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Della --</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688378.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Della Sloane</b> hasn't always had an easy life. Growing up with a mother who barely led her leave the house and have a social life has made her into a girl who's never had a lot of experience with <i>real life</i>. Now, at the age of nineteen, she's finally decided to let go of her fears and start exploring the world. She decides to take a road trip and discover new things she's never tried out before.<br><br><b>"The only thing we have to fear is fear itself."</b><br><br>Della tries to be independent but when she has to make a stop to pump gas, she already encounters her first problem: she doesn't know how to pump gas. Luckily, a very helpful guy named Woods shows up and he teaches her how to do it. The two of them feel an instant spark light up between them and since Della has decided to try new things, she agrees to have dinner with him. A few hours later they end up in Woods's truck and have a night of passionate, steaming hot sex.<br><br><b>"I'd wanted to know what good sex was. Now, I knew what earth shattering sex was. <br>Mission accomplished."</b> ~ Della<br><br>But they both knew it was just a one-night-stand and the next morning Della moves on with her trip. A while later, she ends up working as a waitress at a bar in Dallas with a guy named Tripp. He becomes her friend and when Della has a some problems with their boss and decides she can't keep working their any longer, Tripp offers to let her stay in his empty condo in the coastal town he grew up in and he even fixes her a job with an old friend of his. Turns out this old friend is no one other than Woods Kerrington...<br><br>So, four months after their first encounter, Della ends up working at the Kerrington's Golf Club where Woods is the manager and her newfound boss. It's immediately obvious that there's still an attraction between the two of them and their one night stand might have meant much more than either of them is willing to admit. But, Woods is about to be engaged to a girl his father sat up for him and in order to get a more responsible job at the golf club he has to obey his father's commands. Except, he doesn't have any feelings for this girl. <br><br>Soon, Woods finds himself torn between having to chose between his family and the job he's always dreamed of; and the girl who came rushing into his life and that he hasn't been able to get out of his head ever since.<br><br><b>"My future was about to be completely thrown off track because Della Sloane was under my skin and I had to have her. I couldn't ignore it anymore."</b> ~ Woods<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688379.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~*~<br><br>I really liked Della. She's a girl who's been through so much in her life already, yet she doesn't come over as weak or dependent at all. She's strong and doesn't complain easily and I really admired that about her. She tries to fight her fears and deal with them rather than to run away and hide. No one has ever really cared about her and with Woods she seems to have finally found someone who gave her affection and made all of her problems fade away. Dark secrets from her past still haunt her to this day but Woods is determined to help her get move past them.<br><br><b>"You are mine. Do you hear me? You are mine, Della Sloane. I will take care of you. Nothing is taking you away from me. Nothing."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688380.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Woods, although he certainly isn't perfect and did some things that infuriated me a little, it's kind of hard not to swoon over him. I already loved him in the previous books about Rush and Blaire, but now I LOVE him even more! He's always sweet, responsible, protective and trying to take care of everyone. And well, let's face it, he's HOT. I wouldn't have expected it from him based on what we got to know about him from Rush and Blaire's story but damn, the man has a dirty mouth. And I loved it!!<br><br><b>"I want to be inside you again, Della. I want to pull this sexy ass excuse of a skirt up and bury myself in the tightest pussy I've ever been in."</b><br><br><p>

</p><br><b>"Every time I'm inside of you is making love, baby. <i>Every damn time."</i></b><br><br>At first their relationship is purely based on a physical attraction but after a while, it becomes about much more than that. Once Woods gets to know the <i>real</i> Della, he sees that she's special and worth fighting for. He's never felt that way about anyone before and although Della isn't perfect, neither is he, and it's exactly those imperfections that make them perfect for each other... <br><br><b>"Not everyone sees you the way you do. Sometimes our imperfections are what makes us special."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688382.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"Woods made me whole. He healed everything that was wrong with me. Having him this close to me was all I would ever need."</b> ~ Della<br><br><b>"She's it. No one else. She's all I'm ever gonna want."</b> ~ Woods<br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688383.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br>Although the ending did surprise me a little, I wouldn't exactly call it a cliffhanger. It did end in a way I think will have some major consequences for the rest of the story and that made me very curious what will happen next, but I certainly wouldn't let the ending keep you from giving this first part of the series a try.<br><br>I already know I'll be looking forward to reading much more about Della and Woods in the next part of this enticing series!!!<br><br><br><b>"I don't want to destroy you," she whispered. <br>"Losing you would be the only thing that could destroy me."</b><br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688384.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</p><br><br><br><i>
  <b>"I had a life with Woods to look forward to I knew I could fight whatever darkness that tried to take me. Before Woods I didn't know what I was living for. In my search to find myself, I'd found so much more. I knew now why I wanted to live. I understood love. I had found it."</b>
</i><br><br><br><br><b>4.5 STARS.</b><br><br></span>

<span id="freeTextContainer12734165266469529788"><b>“Not everyone sees you the way you do. Reading his book I fell helplessly in love with him .<br><br>Woods is the rich guy with the arranged future.He cant bare making his own decisions because of his father who controls his life in all domains.Woods must marry Angelica if he wants to run his family bussiness .<br><br><i>How would you feel if you had to marry the most annoying creature in the world?</i><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688387.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Loosing you would be the only thing that could destroy me”</i><br><b>Della</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688388._SY540_.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Della wants to run away from her past and start a new life. The idea of starting a journey with no destination sounds appealing to her and there she meets Woods for the first time.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688389.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After a hot night they part their ways but four months later she ends up working for him.Woods cant forget what happened between them , so seeing her everyday will only f*ck his head.However this atraction between them cant be ignored but hot sex is not the answer to Della's problems.When she is with him she forgets life and she feels like an other person but she cant come between him and his fiancee.<br><br><b>You're engaged and Della is your employee. Draw a line and stay behind it.</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688390.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It hurts him that he cant have her . Being with his fiancee is difficult and their marriage is only going to make him miserable.<br><br><b>All I can think is being with you again.</b><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688391.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Woods doesnt allow his father enforce him marry that shallow girl and he makes the right decision.He doesnt care anymore about the money or the bussiness .He wants to be happy and the only person that makes him happy is Della.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688392.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Della and Woods make the perfect couple.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688393.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688394.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688395.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Sadly no relationship is easy.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688396.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They have to deal with many things.<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688397.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688398.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>All in all , I loved this book . Woods is a man whore and I really like the fact that he changed for a girl. Actually I never thought that he would have a sweet side but he does.Della is an amazing person.She is strong and confident . She is still dealing with her traumas but Woods is there to make her happy and help her move on.<br>Woods' father is so nonchalant and really cold when it comes to his son's happiness.What he did made me wanna punch him . <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Should I be happy that he died?? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The ending<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688399.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm starting to hate cliffhangers.<br><br><b>When I look at you I see life.<br>I see joy.<br>I see future.</b><br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311463ra/688400.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/527354880?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer527354880" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7246261815989920711"><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6fcfba61-77a6-40d3-9531-04aec6a42cc9_zps73bb2f32.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688418.jpg' alt=' photo 6fcfba61-77a6-40d3-9531-04aec6a42cc9_zps73bb2f32.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>I will admit it... I am an Abbi Glines fan girl. She is one of my favorite YA/NA authors. Everything of hers is amazing, so I wasn’t surprised with how much I loved this... It was by far her hottest book to date! And Woods is just too hot to handle!!!!<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/dc512f53-01c7-4e18-a46e-24776f076061_zps878da93d.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688419._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo dc512f53-01c7-4e18-a46e-24776f076061_zps878da93d.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/b327fa5e-5d62-4345-9c45-9d91d15a2dff_zps5e4157ca.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688420.jpg' alt=' photo b327fa5e-5d62-4345-9c45-9d91d15a2dff_zps5e4157ca.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>We all know and love Woods from the ‘Too Far’ series, now lets meet Della...<br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/004316ec-e4ab-430c-b869-c9755c6d374a_zpsf9f80135.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688421.jpg' alt=' photo 004316ec-e4ab-430c-b869-c9755c6d374a_zpsf9f80135.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Della had a very strange and difficult childhood. Her mother had a lot of mental issues, and she was kept indoors a lot. She lived a very sheltered life, an</span>
  <span id="freeText7246261815989920711" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/6fcfba61-77a6-40d3-9531-04aec6a42cc9_zps73bb2f32.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688418.jpg" alt=" photo 6fcfba61-77a6-40d3-9531-04aec6a42cc9_zps73bb2f32.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I will admit it... I am an Abbi Glines fan girl. She is one of my favorite YA/NA authors. Everything of hers is amazing, so I wasn’t surprised with how much I loved this... It was by far her hottest book to date! And Woods is just too hot to handle!!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/dc512f53-01c7-4e18-a46e-24776f076061_zps878da93d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688419._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo dc512f53-01c7-4e18-a46e-24776f076061_zps878da93d.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/b327fa5e-5d62-4345-9c45-9d91d15a2dff_zps5e4157ca.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688420.jpg" alt=" photo b327fa5e-5d62-4345-9c45-9d91d15a2dff_zps5e4157ca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>We all know and love Woods from the ‘Too Far’ series, now lets meet Della...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/004316ec-e4ab-430c-b869-c9755c6d374a_zpsf9f80135.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688421.jpg" alt=" photo 004316ec-e4ab-430c-b869-c9755c6d374a_zpsf9f80135.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Della had a very strange and difficult childhood. Her mother had a lot of mental issues, and she was kept indoors a lot. She lived a very sheltered life, and still has flashbacks and nightmares from her childhood. Della is 19 now. She has her freedom. She recently got her license, and is on the road to find her self, travel, live life. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/3a7f8ad5-0039-4108-a205-befa08a121c3_zps812639f6.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688422.jpg" alt=" photo 3a7f8ad5-0039-4108-a205-befa08a121c3_zps812639f6.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She doesn’t get very far before she has a problem. She doesn’t know how to pump gas, and her car is out. Thankfully, she meets Woods at the gas station. He is more than happy to help her out. Della and Woods go out to dinner that night. After dinner, Della decides to take a chance. Woods is hot, he seems nice, and he wants her. She is not very experienced, but thats what this trip is about. New experiences. No time is wasted... within the first 8% of this book, you will get some smoking hot sex in Woods’ truck. <br><b>
  <blockquote>I’d wanted to know what good sex was. Now, I knew what earth shattering sex was. Mission accomplished.</blockquote>
</b><br>After one earth shattering night, Della is on her way. She lands in Dallas. There, she meets a bartender named Tripp that she becomes friends with. After some problems with her boss, Della leaves Dallas. Tripp offers her to stay at his condo for a while. He knows a guy that can give her a job. Mr. Kerrington. Della accepts, and to her surprise- Mr. Kerrington is Woods.<br><br>Woods is more than a little shocked to see Della several months after their encounter. She has been on his mind. He wants her, but he knows he should stay away. He is getting ready to become an engaged man. He doesn’t want to be, but his father is forcing him if he wants his part of the family business. Woods is pretty torn up about it, but he’s doing what he has to do.<br><b>
  <blockquote>I wasn’t sure if I’d ever be able to forgive him for this. Or maybe it was me I would never be able to forgive. What man let another man control his life? His future?</blockquote>
</b><br>Della isn’t happy about the situation, but she tries to just work for Woods and be his friend. Then, Tripp comes home for a bit. He has feelings for Della and Woods kind of loses it. He wants her no matter what the consequences are. He wants to be there for her, protect her, take care of her. Della is freaked by this. She isn’t the most stable person, she has terrible nightmares, she doesn’t feel good enough for Woods. Woods doesn’t care about any of that. He knows the real Della. He has never felt this way about anyone before. She is it for him.<br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>‘You are mine. Do you hear me? You are mine, Della Sloane. I will take care of you. Nothing is taking you away from me. Nothing.’</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/c3d4bc22-0131-4a10-818a-de2dad614f11_zpscd30fae3.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688423.jpg" alt=" photo c3d4bc22-0131-4a10-818a-de2dad614f11_zpscd30fae3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>LOVED this book! Della is a strong female lead. Even though she has some issues, she is doing the best she can. She is very likable. And oh dear god Woods... In the ‘too far’ books, I had a Rush Crush. This book had me saying Rush who? Woods- loved his kind, sweet, protective, and understanding nature. Staying the night for Della’s nightmares had me seriously swooning. And Woods was so freaking hot... <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/1eeed6b3-b034-4ba9-8c77-a43954d21cab_zpseb09ba37.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688424.jpg" alt=" photo 1eeed6b3-b034-4ba9-8c77-a43954d21cab_zpseb09ba37.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br>Poison's ‘Talk Dirty to Me’ was going through my head for a lot of this book. I loved Wood’s and his dirty mouth. <br><b>
  <i>“I want to be inside you again, Della. I want to pull this sexy ass excuse for a skirt up and bury myself in the tightest pussy I’ve ever been in.”</i>
</b><br>Della and Woods were great together. Loved them as a couple. <br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/363fbc2b-14ff-45ce-8f37-b0a75adc72e7_zpscdf37b56.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688425.jpg" alt=" photo 363fbc2b-14ff-45ce-8f37-b0a75adc72e7_zpscdf37b56.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I’ve heard a lot of people say that this book ended in a cliffhanger- I really didn’t think so... Yes, something big happened at the end, and its something that will effect the next book- but its nothing compared to the Blaire/Rush cliffhanger so don’t let it stop you from reading!<br><br>I really loved this book. I was happy to see a lot of the old crew- and I really liked Tripp... wouldn’t mind if he got a book of his own! Strongly disliked Woods' parents... no surprise there. It was nice to get a Blaire cameo as well. If you liked the ‘Too Far’ series, or if you are an Abbi fan like me, you will LOVE THIS! And if you haven’t read anything by her, what the hell are you waiting for?!?! Her books are awesome. The fall can’t come soon enough... I NEED MORE WOODS!!!<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/Book%20reviews%201/b535f8d0-d9f4-4a15-9c92-942389778bef_zpsff420612.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688426.jpg" alt=" photo b535f8d0-d9f4-4a15-9c92-942389778bef_zpsff420612.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <blockquote>If I had a life with Woods to look forward to I knew I could fight whatever darkeness that tried to take me. Before Woods I didn’t know what I was living for. In my search to find myself, I’d found so much more. I knew now why I wanted to live. I understood love. I had found it.</blockquote>
</b></span>

  <span id="freeText9780105391476297967" style="display:none">SPOILER FREE REVIEW -mature content reader discretion is advised.<br>4 STARS out of 5<br>Genre:New Adult Romance<br><br><b>I am hopelessly in love with Woods! I LOVE-LOVE-LUST HIM!</b><br><br>Dear Woods, I here by give you permission to have your way with me<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688404.jpg" alt=" photo d5eb78f0-271b-4db6-aedb-80f860b9bf5e_zpsddef579a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br> <br>WHOA! I must admit this book surprised me, <b>I did not</b> repeat <b>I did not</b> expect to get the story I read. Nor did I expect the characters to win me over the way they did, just for that I added an extra star to the rating!<br><br><i>‘I was Della Sloane and I was on a road trip to find myself.’</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688405.jpg" alt=" photo 20b53bf89a8385bdc1f1e5e4c1c43057_zpsca5ee0ca.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Della has spent her whole life dealing with her mothers mental instability. Now she spends her nights fighting demons...in her nightmares. While passing through a small coastal town on her road trip, she goes to fill up her gas tank when she suddenly realizes that she has never done so before. She’s only had her license for a few months and in those few months she has never had a car to gas up. While standing at the pump trying to beat back fear of the unkonwn she meets Woods.<br><br><i>“You okay? Need some help?”</i> A deep smooth drawl startled me and I jerked my head around to see a guy smiling at me from the other side of the gas pump. His dark brown eyes appeared to twinkle with laughter as he stared back at me.’<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688406.jpg" alt=" photo brodyjenner3_zps5dd388a0.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After meeting smoking hot Della Sloane at a gas station Woods decides to ask her out to dinner. *Smirks* Dinner leads to mind blowing sex and a one night stand neither of them will ever forget!<br><br>Fast forward four months. Della is back in the small coastal town she once had a night of pleasure in, she is currently looking for a Mr. Kerrington. Her soon to be new boss.<br><br>Greed is twisted, conniving, arrogant and possessive. Greed is a temptress, a temptress with an ugly face. Her face is not what will make you pledge allegiance. No, it is<u> your</u> own desires in <u>your</u> own heart that will trap you. But only if you allow it.<br><br><b>With this ring, I thee wed</b><br>Woods Kerrington finds himself battling for his rightful place in the family business. His father is offering the coveted position of Vice President up on a platter.<b> BUT</b> it comes with a hefty price tag, marriage. His greedy father longs to aline the Kerrington’s with the Greystone’s. If Woods marries the only Greystone heir, Angelina, the union will ensure the two powerhouse families join together.<br><br>Woods struggles on whether or not to bend to his fathers will and finally agrees... Not knowing that Della is about to come back in to his life and put his world on tilt.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688407.jpg" alt=" photo 5f68134b-1a3d-4ffe-adef-e80038061509_zps461692e3.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311463i/688408.jpg" alt=" photo 9b349392-4830-4148-8e7d-0482029cf7d5_zps3e2e9cd8.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>After another mind blowing sexcapade Woods and Della attempt to be friends… Unfortunately they can’t escape the feelings that they have both suppressed for one another.<br><br><br><u>My Thoughts</u><br><b>EXPLOSIVE!</b> That is the best word to describe it! Woods and Della are <b>EXPLOSIVE</b> when they are together. <br>-It did not seem to take long for Woods to figure out that Della was the one for him.<br>-Della’s fear to let another man in after what she had been through was understandable. <br>Both of theses aspects appealed to me as a reader. There was no “I want you” only to turn around and say “I can’t be with you“ and back and forth and so on. Nope. Woods knew he wanted Della he just needed to realize that he was in love and would move MOUNTAINS for her. And thank goodness it did not take the whole book for this realization to take place.*wipes sweat from forehead in relief*<br><br> I felt and knew exactly why Woods wanted the V.P. job; not only was it his birth right but he bust his butt to get it. And his father had the audacity to basically blackmail him. WTF? I wanted to<b> BITCH SLAP</b> his dad. He was a callous prick. And his mother was no better. *sighs sadly* Poor Woods :(<br><br>Della.<i>Della Della Della,</i> this girl has experienced a lot of pain. We get small doses of her sorrow in flashback memories and it is a scary picture that was revealed. I have no idea how one copes with such tragedy or how one deals with a mother so unstable. Thank goodness she had her best friend Braden by her side. Brade is the kind of friend all girls need to have in their corner.<br><br><br>My Ratings<br>Characters- Loved most hated some<br>Writing Style- Good it definitely kept me engrossed in the story<br>Plot/Storyline- Savory and Emotional with some intense flashbacks<br>Steam Factor- High/Very very steamy<br>Overall- I very much enjoyed this story!!!<br><b><br>Now go forth and read. Then come tell us about it on Goodreads!</b><br>For more reviews got to <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogspot.com">http://realitybites-letsgetlost.blogs...</a></span>

<div id="review_536930480" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/536930480" />
    <a title="Jess" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820960-jess"><img alt="Jess" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553552424p2/3820960.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/536930480?book_show_action=true">Feb 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jess" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jess" href="/user/show/3820960-jess">Jess</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820960-jess?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820960-jess?shelf=spin-off">spin-off</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820960-jess?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer536930480" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3262709766476007710"><b>Update: 25/04/2013</b><br/><br/><b>“Is she forever for you then? She's worth throwing it all away?"</b> <b>"She's it. No one else. She's all I'm ever going to want.”</b> -Woods and Grant<br/><br/>Firstly: <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688445.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Secondly: <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688446.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>For those of you that know me, will know that I'm probably Abbi's number one fan...amongst all her other number one fans, so when Donna said we'd be taking part in this blog tour and that I'd get to read Twisted Perfection 2 weeks before release, I did a happy dance. <br/><br/>I've loved all of Abbi's books, and all my expectations</span>
  <span id="freeText3262709766476007710" style="display:none"><b>Update: 25/04/2013</b><br><br><b>“Is she forever for you then? She's worth throwing it all away?"</b> <b>"She's it. No one else. She's all I'm ever going to want.”</b> -Woods and Grant<br><br>Firstly: <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688445.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Secondly: <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688446.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For those of you that know me, will know that I'm probably Abbi's number one fan...amongst all her other number one fans, so when Donna said we'd be taking part in this blog tour and that I'd get to read Twisted Perfection 2 weeks before release, I did a happy dance. <br><br>I've loved all of Abbi's books, and all my expectations were once again fulfilled with Twisted Perfection It's such a wonderful story. I was so excited to read about Woods and Della, two very different people, from different worlds, who meet, fall in love and change each other for the better. As always with Abbi I simply get sucked in from page one, this wasn't any different. I couldn't put this book down and I just kept needing more and more. <br><br>The story was perfectly paced for what needed to be told. The chemistry between Woods and Della is palpable, and you just feel it. This is the thing that I've found with Abbi's books Twisted Perfection included you FEEL everything! You do, you just feel it. Abbi has a way of telling her stories, and it comes out in her writing and it's just wonderful. (This is a gushing review, I'm sorry).<br><br>There were just so many great moments to be had, and I'm so in love with Woods that I honestly didn't know I could love him more than I thought I already did. He's pretty much an Alpha male like more of Abbi's boys are, and he's so fiercely protective of Della, but not in the sadistic way. His and Della's relationship was pretty well thought out, starting from a one night stand, to eventually a chance meeting 4 months on and then eventually falling deeper and deeper in love. It wasn't a slow progression but it wasn't instant either which is great because it totally worked.<br><br>Just going to touch on the ending a little. It was actually pretty perfect, it wasn't an ending I was expecting so it came as a little bit of 'whoa' moment for me; but it was a good ending, most may think it's a cliffhanger, I thought it was to begin with, but on a re-think and having met Abbi personally it's not a cliffhanger it's a nice pause to introduce the 2nd part of their story coming in late Autumn. It'll take you back, but it's worth it.<br><br>I can't really fault anything in Twisted Perfection, I honestly can't, and I don't know if that's because I'm biased because I'm in love with Abbi (such a girl crush) or because there just because I get so enthralled in the story that I completely miss anything off key, I don't know. What I do know is, that Twisted Perfection was a fabulous read, one that I will re-read over and again. I can never get enough of Abbi and her books filled with bad boys and intense passion with hot monkey sex, that I plan to read everything she writes. So if you basically haven't read her Too Far series yet, you should I think pick that up and it's sequel and then read Twisted Perfection. I promise you won't regret it. I anxiously (impatiently) await Woods and Della's sequel Simple Perfection. I. Can't. Wait!<br><br><b>“I loved her. I loved her with a something so fierce I couldn't even name it.”</b> -Woods<br><br><b>“You are mine. Do you hear me? You are mine, Della Sloane. I will take care of you. Nothing is taking you away from me. Nothing.”</b>-Woods<br><br><b>“If I had a life with Woods to look forward to I knew I could fight whatever darkness that tried to take me. Before Woods, I didn’t know what I was living for. In my search to find myself, Id found so much more. I knew now why I wanted to live. I understood love. I had found it.”</b>-Della<br><br>5 mindblowing stars<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688447.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="3262709766476007710" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582825874" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer5288402931553245570"><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“Loosing you would be the only thing that could destroy me”.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/>I love <i>Abbi Glines</i>, she is a great person! But i seem to <b>ALWAYS</b> rate her books 3 stars. <br/>They are 'OK'.<br/>I hoped <i>Twisted Perfection</i> would be different. No such luck.<br/>The only exception ,i think, was <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070903.Fallen_Too_Far__Too_Far___1__Rosemary_Beach___1_' title='Fallen Too Far (Too Far, #1; Rosemary Beach, #1) by Abbi Glines' rel='nofollow noopener'>Fallen Too Far</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13223520.Existence__Existence_Trilogy___1_' title='Existence (Existence Trilogy, #1) by Abbi Glines' rel='nofollow noopener'>Existence</a><br/> <br/>Every one of my friends <b>LOVED</b> this book! I thought i would too.<br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688430.gif' alt='tumblr mc2ui62 SVt1rn95k2o1 500' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>Should have known better.</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688431.gif' alt='tumblr inline mt3t8o BEMD1qj5nlo' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>A 5 star read?</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688432.gif' alt='Ryan Evans Maybe Reaction Gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>A 4 star read?</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688433.gif' alt='Sad nod COLFER' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/app.php' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/><b>More likely.</b><br/><br/><a href='http://postimage.org/' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688434.jpg' alt='c7b3e333 b8cf 4879 bbd6 6c3c61e9d9f2 zps90b91bd7' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><a target='_blank' href='http://postimage.org/' rel='nofollow noopener'></a><br/><br/><br/><br/>Della is on a road trip to find herself, her best friend has jus</span>
  <span id="freeText5288402931553245570" style="display:none"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Loosing you would be the only thing that could destroy me”.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>I love <i>Abbi Glines</i>, she is a great person! But i seem to <b>ALWAYS</b> rate her books 3 stars. <br>They are 'OK'.<br>I hoped <i>Twisted Perfection</i> would be different. No such luck.<br>The only exception ,i think, was <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070903.Fallen_Too_Far__Too_Far___1__Rosemary_Beach___1_" title="Fallen Too Far (Too Far, #1; Rosemary Beach, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen Too Far</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/13223520.Existence__Existence_Trilogy___1_" title="Existence (Existence Trilogy, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Existence</a><br> <br>Every one of my friends <b>LOVED</b> this book! I thought i would too.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688430.gif" alt="tumblr mc2ui62 SVt1rn95k2o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>Should have known better.</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688431.gif" alt="tumblr inline mt3t8o BEMD1qj5nlo" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>A 5 star read?</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688432.gif" alt="Ryan Evans Maybe Reaction Gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>A 4 star read?</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688433.gif" alt="Sad nod COLFER" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>More likely.</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688434.jpg" alt="c7b3e333 b8cf 4879 bbd6 6c3c61e9d9f2 zps90b91bd7" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>Della is on a road trip to find herself, her best friend has just got married, gives her the car and tells her to go and find herself!!<br>On her journey she comes upon a little town in Alabama and meets...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688435.jpg" alt="35562204 410b 4ae0 94dd bee0d5becbda zps8bcbc6f2" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I am in awe of the things you've been put through and the fact you can still light up a room when you walk in. When I look at you I see life. I see joy. I see my future.”</b>
</blockquote> <br><br>Woods has his life planned out - Rise up the ranks of the family business. Marry the rich girl of his parents' dreams.<br> Pretend that wealth and privilege was all he'd ever wanted. <br>But that becomes a little bit complicated when he meets the girl who stirs something deep inside him. <br>Who makes him want something more from life. <br><br><b>Will he cave in? And what will happen when Woods finds out Della has demons that haunt her every night, and that she isn't completely...sane...?</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688436.gif" alt="tumblr mpggjv2r PK1sox2n7o1 400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>In the 1st chapter, we find out that our MC (Della) can not pump gas. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688437.gif" alt="Bitch Please P katherine pierce 18031061 500 28" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>She is 19 and doesn't even know WHERE to put the gas. <br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688438.gif" alt="what everyone was thinking during morgan freeman" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>I know she hasn't been able to go out, and been locked inside. But seriously, i think any person with a tiny bit of brain could figure it out. <br>It's, like, logical. <br><br>I thought she was very dumb. In that moment and throughout the book.<br><br>She was naive and acted a bit like a slut. Went to have sex with strange guys.<br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688439.gif" alt="tumblr lxkb2hj Ty M1qjp4z6o1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br>I am aware that she wants to experience living but does she really have to jump every guy's bones that shows interest in her?<br><br><b>I did not like that.</b><br><br><u>
  <b>Woods.</b>
</u><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688440.gif" alt="tumblr luokd2i ZPu1r21q9ro1 500" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I loved her. I loved her with a something so fierce I couldn't even name it.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Woods was really <b>hot</b>, <b>protective</b> and <b>caring</b>.<br> I really liked him but thought he was a bit of a <b>coward</b>. <br>At times i was like screaming at him to tell his dad to kindly fuck off and let him live his life the way he wants to.<br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Loosing you would be the only thing that could destroy me”.</b>
</blockquote><br><br>BTW - his dad was one selfish, horrible and annoying motherfucker i wanted to punch in the face. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[When he finally died of a heart attack at the end i was like...<br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688441.gif" alt="tumblr lzav5lvqw X1rpwytjo1 400" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br>Serves him right. <br> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688442.gif" alt="black and white fuck off gif Favim com 369553" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Is she forever for you then? She's worth throwing it all away?"<br><br>"She's it. No one else. She's all I'm ever going to want.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>But i really <b>liked where the book was going</b> and <b>occasionally couldn't put it down</b>. <br><b>The plot was good too. <br>I LOVED the writing style. </b><br> <br>It's always like that with Abbi Glines books - <b>she writes beautifully</b> and has <b>good ideas</b>, knows what she's doing. <br>But the <b>characters</b> (especially the female ones) <b>ruin </b>the whole book. <br>They are <b>annoying,</b> <b>naive </b>and make a lot of <b>stupid decisions. </b><br>For me personally they are simply unlikable. <br><br><u>
  <b>Overall...</b>
</u><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688443.gif" alt="yeah ok" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><i>Twisted Perfection</i> was a <b>good read</b>. <br>Not a 4 or 5 star read for sure but quite <b>decent</b>. <br><b>Sexy</b>, <b>short</b>, and <b>interesting.</b><br>Full of <b>romance</b>,<b>heat </b> and <b>drama</b>.<br>If you love <i>Abbi Glines</i> they i suggest you pick it up! <br><b>BUT DO NOT READ THIS IF YOU HAVEN'T READ</b><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/16070903.Fallen_Too_Far__Too_Far___1__Rosemary_Beach___1_" title="Fallen Too Far (Too Far, #1; Rosemary Beach, #1) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Fallen Too Far</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17029526.Never_Too_Far__Too_Far___2__Rosemary_Beach___2_" title="Never Too Far (Too Far, #2; Rosemary Beach, #2) by Abbi Glines" rel="nofollow noopener">Never Too Far</a> <b>THERE ARE SPOILERS. </b><br><br><b>Happy Reading! xxx</b><br><br><a href="http://postimage.org/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688444.gif" alt="Did somebody say vodka" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a target="_blank" href="http://postimage.org/app.php" rel="nofollow noopener"></a><br><br><br><br><b>Thanks Susanne for BR with me! &lt;3</b><br><br><br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/558150793?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Susanne " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Susanne " href="/user/show/7179798-susanne">Susanne </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer558150793" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3116929961337702750"><b>4.5 hot stars!</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688427.gif' width='400' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book made me <b>tingle</b> in all the right places! Abbi Glines has a <i>gift</i>. She makes the story flow and come alive. She doesn't tell me, she <i>
  <b>makes me feel it.</b>
</i> I read it with a goofy smile on my face! <br/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688428._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Della is a broken, strong heroine.</b> She has lived through horrors and she lives with the fear that she has inherited her mother's mental illness. She is giving, caring, beautiful and strong. She is on a road trip to learn how to live. She challenges herself and the world. <br/><blockquote>
  <i>"I am in</i></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText3116929961337702750" style="display:none"><b>4.5 hot stars!</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380311464ra/688427.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book made me <b>tingle</b> in all the right places! Abbi Glines has a <i>gift</i>. She makes the story flow and come alive. She doesn't tell me, she <i>
  <b>makes me feel it.</b>
</i> I read it with a goofy smile on my face! <br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688428._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Della is a broken, strong heroine.</b> She has lived through horrors and she lives with the fear that she has inherited her mother's mental illness. She is giving, caring, beautiful and strong. She is on a road trip to learn how to live. She challenges herself and the world. <br><blockquote>
  <i>"I am in awe of the things you've been put through and the fact you can still light up a room when you walk in. When I look at you I see life. I see joy. I see my future." <i><br></i></i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380311464i/688429.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Woods is the hottie I fell in love with in Fallen too Far. He is <b>sex on a stick.</b> Yum! <br><blockquote>
  <i>Woods was hot, dripping with charisma, and did I mention hot? And I didn’t even know his last name.</i>
</blockquote><b>He made me tingle, blush and swoon.</b> But he has a father who is a royal asshat. The only way Woods can get his promotion is to marry Angelina who is a heiress of the Graystone empire. I loved that we got <i>Wood's perspective</i> in every other chapter! It is the best way to write in first person narration. Yay!<br><br><br>The side cast is wonderful too! Woods friends are <b>one hot bunch!</b> And they all love Della.<br><blockquote>
  <i>"I'm just throwing this out there. I'm making a move on her. Your ass is engaged. So, you can get all pissed and shit but I'm still making a move. She's hot and completely worth the ass kicking." </i>
</blockquote><br>Abbi Glines write sexual chemistry <i>like no one else</i>. <b>My kindle was ready to burst into flames!</b> I could feel Wood’s breath tickle my neck and his hot body invading my space. And there is nothing better than a guy who knows how to <i>
  <b>talk dirty</b>
</i>.<br><blockquote>
  <i>"I want to be inside you again, Della. I want to pull this sexy-ass excuse for a skirt up and bury myself in the tightest pussy I've ever been in."</i>
</blockquote> <br>I have had a lot of misses with NA and it's not my genre – but when I read Abbi Glines I forget it and think I must have been mistaken. It was impossible to put down!<br><br><b>Thank you Sandra for reading it with me! &lt;3 &lt;3 &lt;3</b></span>

<div id="review_526885783" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/526885783" />
    <a title="Jenn" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3349239-jenn"><img alt="Jenn" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1397155775p2/3349239.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/526885783?book_show_action=true">Feb 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jenn" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jenn" href="/user/show/3349239-jenn">Jenn</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3349239-jenn?shelf=accident-coping-death-illness-grief">accident-coping-death-illness-grief</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3349239-jenn?shelf=abroad-roadtrip-travel">abroad-roadtrip-travel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3349239-jenn?shelf=abuse-neglect-serious-content">abuse-neglect-serious-content</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer526885783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1169201681582278096"><b>4 Woods-a-licious Stars</b><br/><br/><b>What I liked about this book:</b><br/>1. I <b>LOVE</b> this cover! Woods is smokin'!!<br/>2. Woods' protectiveness/possessiveness/caring ways for Della<br/>3. Della and Woods' drama doesn't last long<br/>4. This book flows fast<br/>5. Tripp. How can you NOT love this guy?? <br/>6. Woods is a <b>naughty boy</b> in this one ;)<br/>7. <b>Grant</b>-I still have a soft spot for him. <b>Jace</b> is still a good guy. <b>Thad</b> is still an idiot. lol<br/>8. Della- she may have some demons that still haunt her, but she's not a whiny, typical floozy that car</span>
  <span id="freeText1169201681582278096" style="display:none"><b>4 Woods-a-licious Stars</b><br /><br /><b>What I liked about this book:</b><br />1. I <b>LOVE</b> this cover! Woods is smokin'!!<br />2. Woods' protectiveness/possessiveness/caring ways for Della<br />3. Della and Woods' drama doesn't last long<br />4. This book flows fast<br />5. Tripp. How can you NOT love this guy?? <br />6. Woods is a <b>naughty boy</b> in this one ;)<br />7. <b>Grant</b>-I still have a soft spot for him. <b>Jace</b> is still a good guy. <b>Thad</b> is still an idiot. lol<br />8. Della- she may have some demons that still haunt her, but she's not a whiny, typical floozy that cares only about Woods money and what he can do for her. <br /><br /><br /><b>Woods, Woods, Woods...</b> he is stuck with a controlling father in a loveless parent/child relationship with his parents. He is more like a business transaction for his father and does his bidding. His parents, but more actively his father, want him to marry Angelina Greystone so they can link their family business names together. Woods just wants to find happiness, real love and not be forced in to a loveless marriage just for employment gain. He meets Della one night at a gas station when he sees that she's clueless on how to pump gas. They hit it off and eventually he can't get her off his mind. He's got this intense pull to have her, claim her, possess her and keep her safe. This starts the push and need for Woods to change his life around and stop being someone else's puppet. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I'll be whatever she needs me to be. I can't walk away from her, I tried. I'm hooked..."</i>
</b><br /><br /><b>Della, Della, Della...</b> she is emotionally damaged by the life of her crazy mother. She's just barely beginning to figure out who she is and how to live life outside of her home. She has demons that haunt her dreams and words that can trigger things. She seems carefree and unbreakable but in reality, she's fragile deep down. She meets Woods one night before heading to Dallas for a bit. She gets mixed up in a relationship that goes South and her co-worker sends her off to a small coastal town to regroup. Little does she know shes about to meet Woods' BFF and hope for a job at his country club. She is very attracted to Woods and has this intense need to be with him. He's her safe harbor. If she can feel him, hear him and take in his smell it calms her and brings her back to reality.<br /><br />These two go through some bumps together: his parents, her demons, Angelina, and his need to do what he feels is right. Woods was a man <b>POSSESSED</b> and <b> DESPERATE</b> to have Della. <br /><br />I wouldn't say this book ends on a cliffhanger per se... however, I do think the way it ends can wreck havoc on the couple in the next book. Can they weather that storm when faced to deal with it?<br /><br /><b>Examples of Woods needing to claim/possess Della and his desperation:</b><br /><i>"She was curled up on the bed in a small ball. Like she was protecting herself. My hoodie swallowed her but she held it tightly against her just like Tripp had said. Seeing her in my sweatshirt like that had the caveman in me pounding his chest. She was mine."</i><br /><br /><i>"Don't leave me, Della."</i><br /><br /><i>"You are mine. Do you hear me? You are mine, Della Sloane. I will take care of you. Nothing is taking you away from me. Nothing."</i><br /><br /><i> "I love you, Della. I can't lose you. Just you Della. That's all I need. Just you. ..."</i><br /><br /><i>Content: language, drinking, and sexual situations.</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="1169201681582278096" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText17938199140920379507" style="display:none">4 ALL OUT WOODS STARS.<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411436i/808068._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I liked this story LOTS, but I didn't quite get the 5 star feeling. Why? The short answer ~ No book butterflies this time. I've gushed about Abbi Glines before in previous reviews, and YES I'm about to do it again. This author is all about her characters, storyline and her books are like Pringles (once you pop, you just cant stop)! How she grabs me so completely with her story lines - is a mystery.<br><br>This book was a real treat, Abbi one of my BEZZIE authors has created yet again a story of HUGE, likeable proportions. Her writing style is so easy peasy before you know it you've read a whole book and waiting for more ...<br><br>So my thoughts on twisted perfection ...<br>I think we all anticipated we would be ga- ga over Woods, since he stole our hearts in the 'Fallen too Far' series. So it came to no surprise to me that I Loved this character, that's not to say he was delivered without fault - OH NO, there were times I wanted to jump right in my kindle to have a few choice words! With that being said I was sold on his character from the start. Hello, Hot hot HAAAAWT dirty talker. Yes this book delivered hot to the touch STEAM curtesy of our book hero. Our leading heroine is a beautiful package, a young independent woman, dealing with the ghosts of her past and Moving forward with her future. I liked her a lot. I thought there was a Fabulous connection between these two loveables.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411436i/808069._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was a little more gritty and saddening than Glines usual style but I liked it. I felt engaged and connected with the story from page one. As with most of Abbi Glines books she delivers great sub characters, I'm desperado for a book about Tripp and I love how the authors includes friends and family making her stories more complete.<br><br>All in all a big thumbs up from this reader, I'd never let an Abbi Glines book pass me by and I'm more than eager for the follow up to this story, not quite left on a cliff hanger, but close enough to have reader chomping at the bit ... ENJOY GoodReads, mwah.<br><br>4 DONT MISS OUT STARS.</span>

But sadly, it bored me more often then not. I ended up DNF it sadly.<br /><br />Woods has always been the character that stood out for me, bright and shiny, so I really had high hopes for this book.
